// INSPIRATION TUTORIAL //
『靈感』說明=Inspiration
<color\=#FFD145>靈感提升</color>\n{{A}}錄入面具全書後，可以領取靈感點。\n使用靈感點，可以解鎖並提升靈感技能等級。\n\n<color\=#FFD145>靈感重置</color>\n靈感技能可以消耗魂石進行重置。\n重置後返還所有已消耗的靈感點。=<color\=#FFD145>Inspiration</color>\nWith every new Persona recorded in the book, you will earn Inspiration Points, which can be used to unlock and upgrade Wonder's skill tree. More skills and levels are unlocked as you level up further.\n\n<color\=#FFD145>Inspiration Reset</color>\nYou can reset your skill tree by spending Soul Gems, which will return all the Inspiration Points you have used.
